name:M‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äço‚Äç ‚ÄçL‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg
info:Scholars Double Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted May 10, 2024
msg:The gated hotel is a co-op made up of restored and new buildings, a restaurant, and a spa, but nothing over 3 stories. There are numerous restaurants once you leave the grounds -- go west. 

Get the breakfast buffet, it is worth it!

The tourist center is a block west and next to the Grand Canal. Go there, and ask the nice young lady  how to get around. The hotel will give you change for the bus. The police and information will help you in the metro.

Be sure to walk up and down the canal, enjoy people watching, especially the young ladies dressed and made up in beautiful period piece costumes. You can rent one yourself if you wish to participate.

Most of the tourist sights are within walking distance, including the Humble Administer's Garden and the sanpan ride on the canal. The hotel also has a nightly cruise sign up.

If you want to see a panda, you'll have to go to the Taihu Wetland Park -- it's about 30 km from the hotel. You can get there by cab or public transportation.

msg:Suzhou Scholarly Mansion Pingjiang Mansion has a unique geographical location. It is located near Suzhou Pingjiang Historic District. It takes 2 to 3 minutes to walk on the right when you go out. "One Pingjiang Road is half the city of Suzhou." It is also very close to classic attractions: Humble Administrator's Garden, Lion Grove, and Suzhou Museum. The hotel owns a classical private garden with a history of more than 350 years, and has its own attractions: the North Half Garden and the century-old osmanthus tree. Antique charm, pavilions, small bridges and flowing water, autumn scenery, and Jiangnan in dreams are all included here. The 160-year-old sweet-scented osmanthus tree is tall and strong, with lush leaves and flowers. Waves of fragrance swept through the rockery pool in the wind, crossed the white walls and black tiles, and fragrant the surrounding air. The hotel's Chinese restaurant is a local Internet celebrity restaurant. It is ranked No. 1 on the Humble Administrator's Garden gourmet popular list and has been twice recorded on CCTV's "A Bite of China." The classic dishes are very Jiangnan and Suzhou. There was also a Pingtan performance during the banquet, which was full of elegance and uniqueness. The rooms are large in size and have open-air balconies. The interior decoration is elegant and bookish. Tea rhyme pen and paper, it is infinitely enjoyable to calm down and practice calligraphy while sipping tea. For breakfast, you can enjoy Soviet-style pastry snacks and specialty pastries. The service is very good. Whether it is check-in at the front desk, breakfast service, room cleaning or dining in the Chinese restaurant, the service staff are proactive, enthusiastic, polite and thoughtful. Butler Xiaoyu‚Äôs service is very good, special thumbs up! The experience of staying in a characteristic garden-style hotel is very good. Recommended!

msg:If it is the first time to come to Suzhou, bring children and elders, and want to visit various attractions in the old city, then I highly recommend this hotel.

The hotel has the characteristics of Suzhou gardens. The location is superior, quiet amidst the hustle and bustle. You can walk directly to Suzhou Museum, Lion Grove, Humble Administrator's Garden, East Garden, and Coupling Garden. Next door is Pingjiang Road Old Street, Songhe Tower, Weiji Ao Stove noodles, Soochow Su Jin Kee Mung Bean Soup can be eaten whenever you want.
You can also try the Chinese restaurant in the hotel, and you can listen to Pingtan.

But when it comes to the housing experience this time, I don't feel very good. First of all, the parent-child room we booked is located on the first floor of the sky. There are two parent-child rooms, one with a Hello Kitty theme and one with a Doraemon theme. , no actual ventilation effect).

The Doraemon room we stayed in, not to mention the dim lighting in the living room, turned on the air conditioner for two or three hours, which was equivalent to no, and the temperature of nearly 30 degrees was really sweltering. It happened that the HelloKitty room next door was not yet occupied, so I checked that the room was brightly lit. Even without the air conditioner, the temperature was not much different from ours with the air conditioner turned on. Later, after reporting this problem with the lady at the front desk, we arranged for a parent-child room in the Tianci Building. Although the room is bigger, the room on the first floor of Tianci is more suitable for the low-collar segment.

The second point is to talk about the cleanliness of the room. I don‚Äôt know if it‚Äôs because the house was temporarily changed. The floor is still dirty, and some garbage has not been cleaned up. The room is bigger, but there are still a few supplies. For example, facial tissues are only available on the bedside table in the master bedroom. There are too few sockets. There is only one at the head of the bed in the master bedroom, and the rest are under the wall next to the door. Children with low collars should pay attention to safety. In addition, the secondary bathroom is not equipped with hand towels and other supplies. The position where the main bathroom towels are placed needs to climb up the bathtub and step on the edge to get them, which is a bit dangerous. The toothpaste in the children's toothbrush set, the peppermint is so spicy that I don't know what to say. In fact, there are really many places that still need to be improved.

But in the end, I still want to praise the hotel's service. Even if there are more regrets above, one is the lady at the front desk who checked in and solved the stuffy problem of the room for me; the other is room service, because the shower room is not airtight enough , causing the bath water to overflow to the door of the room. She took off her shoes outside the door and came in. She helped us clean up the water and replaced the floor mats and other supplies. The service is very attentive!

msg:I decided to stay in Pingjiang Mansion, a scholarly mansion, largely because of Banyuan‚Äînow this private garden is the back garden of Pingjiang Mansion Hotel. Banyuan is actually the northern half of Suzhou. The location is different from the southern half of Cangmi Lane. It was built during the Shunzhi period and is more than 300 years old. Later, he changed hands to Suzhou Daotai Lu Xiemei, also known as "Lu's Half Garden" in history. Now it belongs to the hotel.
To
Although the entire garden is not big, it is a small house with green jade, with unique landscaping: half pavilions, half corridors, half bridges, and half boats are obvious. The two and a half double eaves attic (the magical appearance is three floors) is not difficult to find, but the owner " The intention of "conten**ent but not perfect" can only be understood by the introduction of Xiao Zhang, a professional tour guide of Pingjiang Mansion. The horizontal plaque hanging in the living room "It's better to live" is also a response to the current mood of the residents. Compared with the Humble Administrator's Garden, the "big man" in Jiangnan gardens not far away, the first surprise of living in Pingjiang Mansion is the elegance of Banyuan, especially the quiet and secret place of morning and evening.
To
The butler at the front desk, Pony Ma, served enthusiastically. Seeing that I was satisfied with my stay, he also delivered jasmine tea. The room service also had a surprise: it could be accompanied by aromatherapy. For dining, you can listen to Pingtan and taste fresh meat mooncakes, squirrel mandarin fish...
